# CATEGORY 1 : FORMAT ALREADY OK -> ONLY TO INSTRUMENT
# CATEGORY 2 : FORMAT ALREADY OK -> NOTHING TO DO
# CATEGORY 3 : FORMAT NOK BUT POSSIBLE TO BE WRITTEN AFTER CONVERSION
# CATEGORY 4 : FORMAT NOK BUT NOT TOP PRIORITY
# CATEGORY 5 : NEVER USED AFTER CONVERSION
# CATEGORY 6 : MESSAGES USED BY SEVERAL TYPEs -> TO DUPLICATE


/MESSAGE/1/TITLE
** ERROR WHILE READING MESSAGE FILE
/MESSAGE/1/DESCRIPTION
   MESSAGE FILE IS EMPTY (NO UNCOMMENTED LINE, COMMENTED LINES START WITH # CHARACTER)
/MESSAGE/1/SOLUTION
   CHECK MESSAGE FILE %s 

/MESSAGE/2/TITLE
** ERROR WHILE READING MESSAGE FILE
/MESSAGE/2/DESCRIPTION
   AN ERROR OCCURRED WHILE READING MESSAGE FILE %s LINE %d
/MESSAGE/2/SOLUTION
   CHECK MESSAGE FILE %s 


/MESSAGE/3/TITLE
** ERROR WHILE READING
/MESSAGE/3/DESCRIPTION
   THERE IS NO DEFINED NODE IN INPUT FILE.
/MESSAGE/3/SOLUTION
    PLEASE DEFINE NODES USING /NODE
    
    
/MESSAGE/5/TITLE
** ERROR IN MATERIAL/PROPERTY CONSISTENCY
/MESSAGE/5/DESCRIPTION
   MATERIAL LAW 19 MUST BE USED WITH /PROP/TYPE9 (ORTHOTROPIC SHELL ELEMENT)
   -- ELEMENT ID: %d
/MESSAGE/5/SOLUTION
   FURTHER INFORMATION ABOUT THIS LAW CAN BE FOUND IN THE RADIOSS THEORY MANUAL

/MESSAGE/503/DESCRIPTION

   -- NODE GROUP TITLE: %s
   THERE ARE %d 10-NODE TETRAHEDRA CONCERNED 
/MESSAGE/503/SOLUTION
   Possible problem when the node group is used in an interface
   and some of the tetrahedra are used to define the main surface
   of an interface type 3, 5, 7, 10 or the secondary surface of an
   interface type 3;
   In such cases, it is recommended to create an external surface from
   the 10-node tetrahedra and to define the secondary node group for the
   interface from the surface.

    2: JETTING AND VENTING FUNCTIONS SHIFTED
        (TTF SHIFT FOR JETTING AND VENTING)
    3: JETTING AND VENTING FUNCTIONS SHIFTED (TTF,TTF+TVENT)
        (TTF SHIFT FOR JETTING TTF+TVENT SHIFT FOR VENTING)
